 2017 main 1,127,167 videshiyon ko america ne green card jari kiya jabaki 2016 main 1,183,505 or 2015 main 1,051,031 logon ko card jari kiya gaya
 The Parliament has passed two such bills that will fundamentally change the way the court appoints judges in the country
 lagata he, sarkaar ne unhen baari jaldbaaji main paarit kiya he
 The government probably wanted to take advantage of the attack on the collegium system from all four sides in the appointment of judges
 lekin is jaldbaaji ke kaaran in vidheyakon main kuch gambhir khamiyaan rah gai hai
 Since 1993, the niche has been under the collegium system appointed by the judges of the court
 is system main varisht jaj hote hai or ve hi jajon kii niyukti karte hai
 But in this system, it was criticized for not saying openness and accountability was not fixed
 in vidheyakon main collegium system kii jagah neshnal juditial epointments kamishan (engeesi) laane kii baat kahi gai he
 The NJAC will have six members: the Chief Justice (CJI), 'two senior judges of the Supreme Court', two 'eminent personalities' and the Law Minister
 isamen ekmaatr rajnatik sadsy ke rup main mantri ko rakhaa gaya he
 Since the 'eminent persons' will be selected by a committee consisting of the Chief Justice and each other against the Prime Minister and the Leader of the Opposition, the 'eminent persons' will probably be independents and impartial
 nae engeesi main teen nyaayik sadsy honge or teen gaiyr-nyaayik sadsy
 No one can object to this equal balance between judicial and non-judicial members
 ab tak desh main nyaayik niyuktiyon kii prakriya ko ekatarfa bataaya jaataa tha, jisamen yaa to karypalika ko nyaaypalika par puri ‘sarvocchata’ hasil hoti thi yaa phir nyaaypalika ko karypalika par
 Thus, in the 1981 First Judges case, the Supreme Court ruled that the executive would have supremacy in the process of judicial appointments, while in 1993 the 'second Judges case' had gained prominence in the judiciary
 ab in nae vidheyakon se jajon kii niyukti main donon ko samaan adhikaar praapt hoga
 However, the current form of NJAC has some serious flaws
 pehali, jo shaayad sabase mahatvapurn he, engeesi main voting kii prakriya sarkaar dwaara kisi bhi samay khatarnaak rup se badali ja sakati he
 Parliament has passed two new laws — the Constitution (99th Amendment) Act, 2014 (which still needs the approval of half of the state legislatures to take effect) and the National Judicial Appointments Commission Act, 2014
 is samay sirf duusare kanoon main hi voting kii prakriya aati he
 It says that the NJAC will appoint judges on the basis of a super-majority of 5-1 — any two members of the NJAC will have the right to veto the appointment of judges
 yah santoshjanak he, kyonki isamen jajon kii niyuktiyon ko ekmaatr rajnatik sadsy yani kanoon mantri kii sahmati ke bina gaiyr-rajnatik banaaya ja saktaa he
 But this system of voting has not been prescribed in the constitutional amendment, but has been laid down in the ordinary law, so it can be changed at any time by the Parliament in times of need
 desh main nyaayik niyuktiyon ke maamle main samvidhan ke praavdhaanon main sanshodhan karnaa aasaan nahin he
 This requires a two-thirds majority in Parliament and approval from the state legislatures
 iske vipareet saadhaaran kanoon sansad main saadhaaran bahumat se paarit kiye ja sakate hai
 Thus the law on the Judicial Appointments Commission can be changed at any time through a simple majority of Parliament
 doosraa, engeesi bahut zyada kendrikrut he
 In the collegium system, the local high court collegiums play a major role in the appointment of high court judges
 iske vipareet engeesi puri tarah kendriya sanstha he, jisamen sthaneey pratinidhitiv ke liye koi sthaan nahin he
 Aware of the ground realities of their states, the Chief Justices of the High Court have no role in the NJAC
 iske alaava, kendriya mantri ko yah faisla karne kaa adhikaar kyon praapt hona chahie ki madras hycourt main koun jaj hoga
 The new law requires NJAC to consider only the recommendations of the High Court Chief Justices and state governments, but those recommendations can be completely ignored
 is par koi roak nahin he
 Third, although the system of judicial appointments has changed, people are apprehensive that there may be a change in the traditional way of judicial appointments
 is samay ye alikhit niyam hai ki 55 saal se kam umr ke vyakti ko supreme court kaa jaj nahin niyukti kiya ja saktaa he or sirf ‘varisht’ jaj (zyaadaatar hycourt ke mukhya nyaayadhish) hi supreme court ke jaj ban sakate hai
 Whereas merit should be considered as the basis, not age and seniority
 engeesi main is chalan ko badalane kii koi vyavastha nahin he
 If such a system were put in place, then relatively energetic, qualified and young judges would also get a chance to appear in the Supreme Court
 in vidheyakon ke saath kuch or bhi samasyaayein hai
 The 99th Constitution Amendment does not clarify whether the President is obliged to comply with the recommendations of the NJAC
 iske alaava, pradhan nyaayadhish ke chayan main engeesi main gaiyr-nyaayik sadasyon kaa bahumat he
 In short, although some reforms were needed in the collegium system, there are many serious mistakes in the hastily drafted bills, which need to be looked into deeply
 aise main jarurat is baat kii he ki sarkaar is kanoon ko pratishtha kaa prashn banane kii bajaae ek behatar kanoon banane ke bare main soche
 It would be better for the basic spirit of the Constitution and for the freedom of all the basic pillars of democracy
